	id = ZES_soup_kitchens
	icon = GFX_goal_food_problem2
	x = -6
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = ZES_lua_ramedi_elected
	cost = 5.80
	prerequisite = { focus = ZES_expand_literacy_campaign }

	available = {
		has_government = democratic
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Get.Date.Text]: [Root.GetName]: ZES_formalize_book_drives"
		custom_effect_tooltip = ZES_xatisa_relief_tp
		add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.10 }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ZES_xatisa
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = ZES_xatisa
					add_idea = ZES_xatisa_lua_1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ZES_xatisa_lua_1
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = ZES_xatisa_lua_1
					add_idea = ZES_xatisa_lua_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ZES_xatisa_lua_2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = ZES_xatisa_lua_2
					add_idea = ZES_xatisa_lua_3 
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = ZES_xatisa_lua_3 
					add_idea = ZES_xatisa_lua_4
				}
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = ZES_air_9
	icon = GFX_goal_arms_dealing
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = { focus = ZES_air_6 focus = ZES_air_7 }
	relative_position_id = ZES_air_2
	x = 0
	y = 3

	available = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone" }

			has_tech = basic_small_airframe

			else = {
				OR = {
					has_tech = fighter1
					has_tech = CAS1
					has_tech = naval_bomber1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 70
	}

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ZES_air_9"
		custom_effect_tooltip = ZES_air_focus_tp
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone" }

			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "Kobri"
				type = small_plane_airframe_1
				modules = {
					fixed_main_weapon_slot = light_mg_4x
					engine_type_slot = engine_1_1x
					special_type_slot_1 = empty
				}
				icon = "GFX_ZES_fighter1_medium"
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = small_plane_airframe_1
				amount = 75
				producer = ZES
				variant_name = "Kobri"
			}

			if = {
				limit = { has_tech = early_bombs }

				create_equipment_variant = {
					name = "Janelas"
					type = small_plane_cas_airframe_1
					modules = {
						fixed_main_weapon_slot = small_bomb_bay
						engine_type_slot = engine_1_1x
						special_type_slot_1 = empty
					}
					icon = "GFX_ZES_CAS1_medium"
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = small_plane_cas_airframe_1
					amount = 50
					producer = ZES
					variant_name = "Janelas"
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = { has_tech = basic_torpedo }

				create_equipment_variant = {
					name = "Murgudjador"
					type = small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_1
					modules = {
						fixed_main_weapon_slot = torpedo_mounting
						engine_type_slot = engine_1_1x
						special_type_slot_1 = empty
					}
					icon = "GFX_ZES_naval_bomber1_medium"
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_1
					amount = 50
					producer = ZES
					variant_name = "Murgudjador"
				}
			}

			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_tech = fighter1 }
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = small_plane_airframe
						amount = 75
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_tech = CAS1 }
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = small_plane_cas_airframe
						amount = 50
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_tech = naval_bomber1 }
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = 	small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe
						amount = 50
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
